RECENT CHANGES — 2026-04-16 (Wave 3, prompt 06/20)
--------------------------------------------------

Hybrid domain reconstruction: domain detection now fuses four signals
(topical embeddings, premise Jaccard overlap, ontology entity hits,
normative-axis cosine) into a weighted `DomainMix`. The legacy
`DomainDetector.detect()` single-domain API is unchanged; the hybrid
path is a brand-new `detect_domain_mix()` function.

  - MOD  core/types.py  (new frozen `NormativeProfile` with rights/
         utilitarian/deontic axes, new frozen `DomainMix` with
         weights tuple, normative profile, optional ontology_graph_id,
         optional notes tuple, schema_version "domain-mix-v1", and a
         `top()` convenience accessor returning the highest-weight
         entry or None).
  - NEW  server/fund/data/normative_markers.json
         (lemma lists per normative axis; schema_version
         "normative-markers-v1").
  - NEW  domain/normative.py
         (`compute_normative_profile(propositions) -> NormativeProfile`;
         normalized lexical frequency per axis with [0, 1] clamp;
         bundled-JSON lexicon with safe defaults on IO/JSON errors).
  - MOD  domain/premises.py
         (adds module-level `DOMAIN_NORMATIVE` table with declared
         (rights, utilitarian, deontic) triples for all 10 domains,
         plus `get_domain_normative(key)` helper that falls back to
         (0.33, 0.33, 0.33); existing DOMAINS/TENSIONS untouched).
  - MOD  domain/detector.py
         (adds `detect_domain_mix(propositions, ontology, *, embedder,
         top_k)`; legacy DomainDetector class untouched. Per-domain
         score is
         `0.4*w_topic + 0.25*w_premise + 0.2*w_ontology + 0.15*w_normative`;
         w_topic uses SBERT-or-TF-IDF cosine between mean proposition
         embedding and per-domain premise centroids; w_premise is
         stopword-filtered Jaccard on content lemmas; w_ontology is
         normalized count of ontology entity surface forms that match
         domain premise keywords by word boundary; w_normative is
         cosine between the argument's NormativeProfile and each
         domain's declared profile. Any signal that cannot compute
         (missing embedder, empty ontology, empty text, empty arg
         normative vector, etc.) is skipped, its coefficient is
         redistributed across surviving signals, and a
         "signal_skipped: <name>" string is appended to the DomainMix
         `notes` tuple. Final per-domain scores are sorted desc,
         top_k is clamped to at least 1, and weights are renormalized
         to sum to 1.0. When every signal is skipped, the returned
         DomainMix has empty weights and populated notes. The
         ontology_graph_id is a stable sha256-prefix fingerprint of
         the ontology entities+edges or None for empty ontologies.
         Comparator is untouched; DomainMix.top() is available for
         callers that want a single (domain, weight) pair).
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/hybrid_domain/rights_argument.json
         (4-proposition rights-leaning fixture).
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/hybrid_domain/market_argument.json
         (4-proposition market-leaning fixture).
  - NEW  tests/test_hybrid_domain.py
         (12 tests: legacy single-domain API preservation, rights-
         fixture produces a valid DomainMix with weights summing to
         1.0 and descending order, determinism across repeat calls
         with fresh TF-IDF embedders, TF-IDF fallback yields market_
         economics in the top-k for the market fixture, empty
         OntologyGraph adds `signal_skipped: ontology` note, `None`
         ontology also skips, weights-sum-to-1 invariant across
         top_k in {1, 2, 3, 5}, empty propositions path returns empty
         weights plus all four `signal_skipped` notes, DomainMix.top()
         returns the highest-weight entry, ontology_graph_id is a
         16-character string when the ontology has entities,
         compute_normative_profile puts rights-heavy text above the
         utilitarian axis, and empty-input normative profile is all
         zeros).

No new runtime dependencies. domain/comparator.py is intentionally
unchanged; callers that want a single-domain handoff can use
`DomainMix.top()`.

Verification:
  python3 -m pytest tests/test_hybrid_domain.py -v   # 12 passed
  python3 -m pytest tests/ --deselect tests/test_scorer.py::TestContradictoryText::test_contradictory_pitch -q
    # 492 passed, 3 skipped, 1 deselected
  python3 -c "from coherence_engine.domain.detector import detect_domain_mix; print('ok')"
  # -> ok


RECENT CHANGES — 2026-04-17 (Wave 5, prompt 13/20)
--------------------------------------------------

- New `server/fund/services/red_team.py` implements the adversarial
  regression harness:
    * `run_adversarial_suite(fixtures_dir, labels_path,
      policy_version)` loads the labeled fixture corpus, replays each
      case end-to-end through `ScoringService.score_application(...)` +
      `DecisionPolicyService.evaluate(...)` (the same chain used by
      `ApplicationService.process_next_scoring_job`), translates the
      decision-policy `fail` -> `reject` canonicalization, and returns
      a `RedTeamReport` (`schema_version=red-team-report-v1`) with
      total / matches / mismatches counters,
      `false_pass`/`false_reject`/`false_review`, a 3 x 3
      `confusion_matrix` keyed by `expected_verdict` ->
      `actual_verdict`, and a `cases` list with per-fixture details
      (CI95, anti-gaming flags, failed gate codes, threshold required,
      coherence observed, margin).
    * `to_canonical_bytes()` serializes with `sort_keys=True` and
      fixed separators so consecutive runs are byte-identical
      (asserted in tests).
    * `RedTeamError` carries operator-readable messages for every
      load/schema failure surface (missing dir, missing labels,
      malformed JSON, unknown verdict, unknown category, missing
      label for a fixture, policy-version pin mismatch).
- Adversarial corpus seeded under `tests/adversarial/`:
    * 12 fully synthetic fixtures (no real founders/companies, no
      PII): 4 incoherent, 4 coherent + evidenced, 2 template-echo, 2
      borderline. Domain coverage spans `market_economics`,
      `public_health`, and `governance`. One incoherent fixture sets
      `compliance_status="blocked"` to exercise the hard-fail
      compliance path; one borderline fixture sets
      `compliance_status="review_required"` to exercise the
      manual-review compliance path.
    * `labels.json` maps each fixture filename to
      `{expected_verdict, rationale}`. `expected_verdict` is the
      canonical external vocabulary
      (`pass | reject | manual_review`).
- New CLI verb `red-team-run --fixtures-dir <dir> --labels <file>
  [--output <file>] [--policy-version <pin>]`. Prints the canonical
  JSON report to stdout (mirroring to disk when `--output` is given).
  Exit `0` if every fixture's actual verdict matches its label, `1`
  if at least one mismatch is recorded, `2` on fixture / labels load
  failure or policy-version pin mismatch (per-prompt-13 contract).
- Tests: `tests/test_red_team_harness.py` — 19 cases pinning the
  current confusion matrix against the 12 fixtures
  (`pass`->`reject`: 4, `reject`->`reject`: 4, `manual_review`->
  `reject`: 4; `matches=4`, `mismatches=8`, `false_reject=8`,
  `false_pass=0`, `false_review=0`) so any drift in the scorer,
  anti-gaming detector, decision-policy thresholds, or
  fail->reject canonicalization fails the suite loudly. Hygiene
  cases assert (a) >= 12 fixtures present, (b) all four required
  categories represented at the prescribed counts, (c) every
  fixture has a label, (d) every label verdict is canonical, (e)
  the report is byte-deterministic across consecutive runs, (f)
  every `RedTeamError` surface raises (missing fixtures dir,
  missing labels, policy-version pin mismatch, unlabeled fixture,
  unknown verdict in labels). Three CLI smokes shell out to
  `python -m coherence_engine red-team-run` and assert exit `1`
  on the current mismatch baseline, exit `2` on missing fixtures
  dir + on policy-version pin mismatch, and exit `0` when labels
  are aligned to the currently observed actual verdicts via a
  tmp-path `labels_aligned.json`.
- New spec `docs/specs/red_team_harness.md` documents fixture
  authoring (required fields, four categories, name/PII
  prohibitions), the canonical verdict vocabulary, per-case +
  aggregate report schema, CLI exit codes, determinism guarantees
  (`tfidf` embedder + heuristic contradiction backend, sorted
  filename iteration, no DB writes), and a step-by-step "bumping
  the pin" workflow for intentional behavior changes (regenerate,
  document, link PR).
- Prohibitions honored:
    * No fixture identifies a real founder or company
      (synthetic-only names: Meridian Analytics, Orchid Care, Civic
      Beacon, Tidewater Logistics, Polaris Health, Larkfield
      Robotics, Stratos Cloud, Helix AI, Nimbus Ledger,
      Brightspoke).
    * The harness performs zero network I/O (it uses only the
      `tfidf` embedder + `heuristic` contradiction backend already
      configured by `ScoringService`); tests are intentionally NOT
      marked network-dependent.
    * Only files listed in SCOPE were created or modified
      (`server/fund/services/red_team.py`, `cli.py`,
      `tests/test_red_team_harness.py`, `tests/adversarial/...`,
      `docs/specs/red_team_harness.md`, STATUS, CONTINUATION).

Verify with:
  cd Coherence_Engine_Project
  python3 -m pytest coherence_engine/tests/test_red_team_harness.py -v
  python3 -m coherence_engine red-team-run \
    --fixtures-dir coherence_engine/tests/adversarial/fixtures \
    --labels coherence_engine/tests/adversarial/labels.json \
    --output /tmp/ce-redteam.json
  # exit 1 (8 mismatches against current pinned baseline)


RECENT CHANGES — 2026-04-17 (Wave 4, prompt 12/20)
--------------------------------------------------

- Added a per-application `scoring_mode` column on `Application`
  (`String(16)`, NOT NULL, `server_default "enforce"`) with values
  `enforce | shadow`. Existing rows default to `enforce`, preserving
  production behavior.
- New Alembic migration
  `alembic/versions/20260417_000004_scoring_mode.py` (revision
  `20260417_000004`, down_revision `20260417_000003`) adds the column
  idempotently (no-op when it already exists) and uses
  `batch_alter_table` on downgrade for SQLite compatibility.
- `ApplicationService.process_next_scoring_job` now branches on the
  application's `scoring_mode`:
    * `enforce` (default): unchanged — `kind="decision_artifact"` row
      persisted via `persist_decision_artifact`; `DecisionIssued`
      event carries `mode="enforce"`.
    * `shadow`: the same deterministic `decision_artifact.v1` bundle is
      built + validated but persisted as
      `kind="shadow_decision_artifact"` through a new
      `_persist_shadow_decision_artifact` helper;
      `DecisionIssued` carries `mode="shadow"`; founder-facing
      notification side effects are suppressed (the
      `_handle_transcript_rejection` path skips the `FounderNotified`
      publish when the application is in shadow mode).
- `ApplicationService.create_escalation_packet` rejects partner
  escalation packets for shadow-mode applications with
  `escalation_forbidden_in_shadow_mode` — no partner-facing side
  effects are ever produced under shadow.
- New `ApplicationService.set_scoring_mode(application_id, *,
  new_mode, force=False)` method: validates the target mode, treats
  same-mode as a no-op, and refuses `enforce -> shadow` after a
  decision has been issued unless `force=True`. `shadow -> enforce`
  (promote-after-review) is always allowed.
- `server/fund/services/event_publisher.py` now exports
  `SCORING_MODE_ENFORCE`, `SCORING_MODE_SHADOW`,
  `tag_payload_with_mode(payload, mode)`, and
  `is_shadow_event_payload(payload)` so both the application service
  and downstream dispatchers share one vocabulary for event mode
  tagging.
- Event schema `server/fund/schemas/events/decision_issued.v1.json`
  gains an OPTIONAL `mode` property (`enum = ["enforce", "shadow"]`,
  default `"enforce"`). It is NOT added to `required`, so all pre-
  prompt-12 events validate unchanged.
- New CLI verb: `application set-mode --application-id <id> --mode
  enforce|shadow [--force]`. Prints a JSON result with
  `application_id`, `previous_mode`, `new_mode`, `changed`. Exits
  `2` on validation failure (missing application, forbidden
  `enforce -> shadow` without `--force`, unknown mode).
- Tests: `tests/test_shadow_mode.py` — 22 cases covering model
  defaults + shadow persistence, event-publisher mode helpers, all
  six `set_scoring_mode` transition branches, end-to-end worker
  runs proving shadow yields a `shadow_decision_artifact` row (and

  `mode="shadow"`, no `FounderNotified` is enqueued, escalation is
  blocked, and CLI smokes for happy-path, forbidden transition
  (exit 2), `--force` override, missing application (exit 2), and a
  shadow -> enforce round trip.
- Prohibitions honored: `decision_issued` event is NOT renamed or
  dropped (schema only gains an optional field); enforce-mode
  notification side effects are NOT silently swallowed (suppression
  is gated strictly on `scoring_mode == "shadow"` with coverage);
  only files listed in SCOPE were modified, plus
  `decision_issued.v1.json` which the step-by-step explicitly
  directs as a normative update.

RECENT CHANGES — 2026-04-16 (Wave 2, prompt 09/20)
--------------------------------------------------

Deterministic anti-gaming detector wired into the composite scoring path.
Produces `anti_gaming_score ∈ [0,1]` (1.0 = clean) plus a list of flag
codes and audit metrics. Applied as a bounded composite-stage adjustment
`composite = raw_composite * (0.5 + 0.5 * anti_gaming_score)` — clean
arguments are unchanged; the worst case halves the composite. Zero new
runtime dependencies (stdlib only).

  - NEW  core/anti_gaming.py  (`AntiGamingReport(score, flags, metrics)`,
         `detect_anti_gaming(propositions, *, prior_corpus=(),
         templates=())`, module-level flag-code constants
         `AG_TEMPLATE_OVERLAP` / `AG_REPETITIVE_FILLER` /
         `AG_PRIOR_CORPUS_ECHO` / `AG_FLUENCY_WITHOUT_CONTENT` /
         `AG_CONTRADICTION_DENIAL`, and a `FLAG_WEIGHTS` mapping with
         weights 0.30 / 0.20 / 0.25 / 0.15 / 0.25 documented in the
         module docstring. Signals are all offline lexical/numeric:
         char-trigram Jaccard for template + prior-corpus echoes,
         length-normalized sublinear-TF cosine for self-similarity
         saturation — stdlib only, no sklearn — ratio of long+complex
         propositions to metric/numeric-bearing propositions for the
         fluency-vs-content gap, and per-sentence negation +
         content-token repetition without a concession marker for
         contradiction denial).
  - MOD  core/scorer.py  (additive: new keyword-only `anti_gaming=True`
         with optional `prior_corpus=()` / `templates=()` on
         `CoherenceScorer.score(...)`. When enabled, runs the detector
         over `structure.propositions` and applies the bounded
         multiplier to the raw composite. `CoherenceResult.metadata`
         gains `raw_composite_score`, `anti_gaming_score`,
         `anti_gaming_flags`, `anti_gaming_metrics`. Graceful
         degradation: detector exceptions are logged verbosely and
         fall back to a clean (multiplier=1.0) default so scoring
         never fails on anti-gaming issues. The early-return path for
         `n_propositions < 2` also fills these metadata keys with
         clean defaults for shape stability downstream).
  - MOD  server/fund/services/scoring.py  (`anti_gaming_score` is now
         sourced from the detector via the scorer's metadata instead of
         the previous contradiction-count heuristic; adds
         `anti_gaming_flags` and `anti_gaming_metrics` to the returned
         dict. The sign convention is now the canonical clean-score
         convention 1.0=clean).
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/anti_gaming/clean.json  (no flags expected).
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/anti_gaming/template_echo.json  (one
         proposition is a near-verbatim template copy).
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/anti_gaming/repetitive.json  (near-identical
         propositions → self-similarity > 0.85).
  - NEW  tests/test_anti_gaming.py  (12 cases: clean fixture yields
         no flags and score==1.0, `AG_TEMPLATE_OVERLAP` trigger on
         template echo, `AG_REPETITIVE_FILLER` trigger on repetitive
         fixture, synthetic prior-corpus echo triggers
         `AG_PRIOR_CORPUS_ECHO`, empty propositions yield a clean
         report, detector is byte-deterministic across calls,
         bounded-penalty property `composite >= 0.5 * raw_composite`,
         clean pitch preserves composite (multiplier==1.0),
         `anti_gaming=False` disables penalty and records clean
         defaults, flag-weight shape invariant, and
         `ScoringService.score_application(...)` passes the three
         fields through to the return dict).

Verification:
  PYTHONPATH=.. python3 -m pytest tests/test_anti_gaming.py -v      # 12 passed
  PYTHONPATH=.. python3 -m pytest tests/ --deselect tests/test_scorer.py::TestContradictoryText::test_contradictory_pitch -q
    # 532 passed, 3 skipped, 1 deselected
  PYTHONPATH=.. python3 -c "from coherence_engine.core.anti_gaming import detect_anti_gaming; print('ok')"
  # -> ok

Note: `server/fund/services/decision_policy.py` was intentionally left
untouched (out of scope). Its existing anti-gaming gate thresholds
(`anti_gaming_warn_min=0.25`, `anti_gaming_max=0.35`) were authored
against the placeholder "risk-score" convention in the previous
`scoring.py` heuristic. A follow-up prompt will re-threshold those gates
against the canonical clean-score convention; the existing unit tests
for `DecisionPolicyService` still pass because they pass `anti_gaming_score`
values as hardcoded dict inputs rather than via the scorer.


RECENT CHANGES — 2026-04-16 (Wave 1, prompt 08/20)
--------------------------------------------------

Versioned prompt registry with SHA pinning. Every LLM prompt now has a
stable id, semver version, owner, status ({draft, shadow, prod}), and the
SHA-256 of its body file's raw bytes. A stable registry digest is exposed
via CLI so the decision artifact's `pins.prompt_registry_digest` is
reproducible and auditable.

  - NEW  data/prompts/registry.json
         (schema_version `prompt-registry-v1`, two seed prod entries:
         `interview_opening` v1.0.0 and `self_critique` v1.0.0, both
         owned by `fund-ops`; `content_sha256` values match the bytes on
         disk exactly).
  - NEW  data/prompts/bodies/interview_opening.v1.md
         (founder-voice interview opening prompt template).
  - NEW  data/prompts/bodies/self_critique.v1.md
         (self-critique prompt template with structured JSON output schema).
  - NEW  server/fund/services/prompt_registry.py
         (`load_registry`, `verify_registry`, `registry_digest`,
         `resolve`, `default_registry_path`, `iter_entries`, dataclasses
         `PromptEntry`/`Registry`/`Mismatch`/`VerificationReport`,
         `PromptRegistryError`. Digest is SHA-256 over a JSON-encoded
         sorted list of `(id, version, content_sha256)` tuples —
         deterministic, order-insensitive to declaration order, and
         version-sensitive. Content hashing is over raw on-disk bytes
         only — no normalization or stripping).
  - MOD  cli.py
         (new `prompt-registry` subcommand group with verbs `list`,
         `verify`, `digest`; each accepts `--registry <path>`;
         `list`/`verify` accept `--json`; verification failure exits 2
         matching the parity convention set by
         `validate-historical-export`).
  - NEW  tests/test_prompt_registry.py  (17 cases: load/parse, verify OK
         on fresh fixtures, body-mutation detection, missing-body
         reporting, digest determinism across calls, digest
         order-insensitivity, digest changes when a content SHA changes,
         resolve hit/miss, schema/status/duplicate rejection, shipped
         registry self-verifies, and four CLI subprocess smokes —
         `verify` exit 0 on good state, `list` prints seeded entries,
         `digest` emits a valid hex sha256, and `verify` exit 2 on a
         tampered out-of-tree fixture).
  - NEW  docs/specs/prompt_registry.md  (schema, digest semantics,
         draft->shadow->prod lifecycle, CLI verb table, invariants).

No new runtime dependencies. Prompt bodies are never embedded inline in
the JSON — the registry only references them via `body_path`.

Migration note: pre-existing migrations 20260409_000002 and 20260409_000004
contain `op.alter_column(..., server_default=None)` calls that are not valid
SQLite syntax. Hosted environments typically run alembic against
PostgreSQL/MySQL (where these calls succeed); local SQLite test runs use
`Base.metadata.drop_all/create_all` via `tests/test_decision_artifact.py`
and other fund-test fixtures. The new `20260417_000002_artifact_kind.py`
migration is SQLite-safe and verified against a fresh schema (stamped to
`20260417_000001`, then upgraded and downgraded cleanly).

================================================================================
  WAVE 7 — POSTGRES PARITY AUDIT (prompt 21 of 70)
================================================================================

Postgres parity audit + SQLite-to-Postgres migration registry. Audit only;
defective migrations are rewritten in prompt 24.

  - NEW  deploy/scripts/audit_migrations_postgres_parity.py
         AST-based auditor over `alembic/versions/`. Flags
         `op.alter_column(..., server_default=None)` (sqlite-incompatible
         error), naked NOT NULL `sa.Boolean` columns without
         `server_default` (warning), `op.execute(...)` SQL with PRAGMA or
         out-of-place `IF NOT EXISTS` (postgres-incompatible error),
         `op.batch_alter_table(...)` (recorded as
         `sqlite_only_pattern_batch_alter_table`, NOT a defect), and
         `op.create_foreign_key` without a follow-up
         `ALTER TABLE ... NOT VALID` (warning). Exit 0 when every
         revision has `errors == []`, else exit 2. Never wall-clock —
         `audited_at` is taken from `git log -1 --format=%aI`.
  - NEW  data/governed/migration_registry.json
         (`schema_version: "migration-registry-v1"`). Current state:
         10 revisions audited; 6 errors across 2 revisions
         (20260409_000002 and 20260409_000004) all of code
         `alter_column_server_default_none_sqlite`; 7 warnings
         (3 `boolean_no_server_default`, 4
         `sqlite_only_pattern_batch_alter_table`).
  - MOD  cli.py
         New top-level verb `db audit-migrations
         [--write-registry] [--versions-dir PATH] [--registry-path PATH]
         [--json] [--audited-at ISO]`. Delegates to the auditor; exit
         status mirrors the underlying script.
  - NEW  docs/specs/migration_registry.md
         Full spec for the registry + audit rule table. Lists the
         convention that any revision running against Postgres in CI
         must have `errors == []`.
  - NEW  tests/test_migration_registry.py
         10 tests: synthetic-fixtures-match-pinned-JSON, per-rule
         single-revision tests, real-tree regression test against
         `tests/fixtures/migrations/real_audit_baseline.json` (pins
         current error/warning counts), CLI exit-code tests for both
         the dirty real tree and a clean fixture-only tree, and a
         schema-version sanity check on the committed registry.
  - NEW  tests/fixtures/migrations/{20260101_000001_clean.py,
         20260101_000002_alter_default_none.py,
         20260101_000003_naked_boolean.py,
         20260101_000004_batch_alter.py, expected_registry.json,
         real_audit_baseline.json}.

================================================================================
  WAVE 7 — SUPABASE POSTGRES CONNECTION + RLS SCAFFOLD (prompt 22 of 70)
================================================================================

Dialect-aware database connection layer + declarative Row-Level-Security
policy registry and migration. SQLite remains the default for unit tests
and CI; Postgres / Supabase paths are now first-class.

  - MOD  server/fund/database.py
         New `resolve_database_url(env)` walks the resolution order
         `DATABASE_URL` > `SUPABASE_DB_POOLER_URL` > `SUPABASE_DB_URL` >
         `COHERENCE_FUND_DATABASE_URL` > `sqlite:///./coherence_fund.db`.
         Appends `?sslmode=require` when the URL targets a
         `*.supabase.co` / `*.supabase.com` host (existing `sslmode`
         values are preserved). New `_engine_kwargs_for_url(url)`
         returns dialect-appropriate engine kwargs:
           - SQLite: `connect_args={"check_same_thread": False}`.
           - Direct Postgres: `pool_size=10, max_overflow=20,
             pool_pre_ping=True, pool_recycle=1800`.
           - Supabase pgbouncer pooler (host contains `pooler` or
             `pgbouncer=true` query param): `poolclass=NullPool` with
             `pool_pre_ping=True` so SQLAlchemy does not pool on top of
             pgbouncer transaction-mode. New `safe_url_for_logging(url)`
             returns `<dialect>://<user>@<host>:<port>/<db>` (passwords
             stripped) for log-safe rendering.
  - MOD  server/fund/config.py
         New optional settings: `DATABASE_URL_EXPLICIT`,
         `SUPABASE_DB_POOLER_URL`, `SUPABASE_DB_URL`,
         `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`. Legacy `DATABASE_URL` field is
         preserved (Alembic env still reads it; existing tests still
         mutate it).
  - NEW  server/fund/security/rls.py
         Declarative `RLSPolicy` dataclass (`table`, `name`, `command`,
         `using_clause`, `with_check_clause`, `roles`) + `RLS_POLICIES`
         registry covering `fund_applications`, `fund_decisions`,
         `fund_event_outbox`, `fund_idempotency_records`, and
         `argument_artifacts`. Every protected table has a
         `service_role ALL` policy; founder-scoped tables additionally
         have `authenticated SELECT` policies gated on
         `auth.uid() = founder_user_id` (column lands in prompt 25).
         `apply_rls_policies(connection, policies)` issues
         `ALTER TABLE ... ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY` then
         `DROP POLICY IF EXISTS` + `CREATE POLICY` for each policy on
         Postgres; no-op on SQLite (and any non-Postgres dialect).
         `revert_rls_policies(...)`, `render_policy_ddl(...)`,
         `rls_tables(...)` round out the public surface.
  - MOD  server/fund/security/  (package conversion)
         Former `server/fund/security.py` is now `security/middleware.py`;
         `security/__init__.py` is a lazy `__getattr__` shim that
         forwards attribute access to `.middleware`. Existing
         `from coherence_engine.server.fund.security import X` imports
         continue to work; importing `security.rls` no longer drags in
         FastAPI/pydantic.
  - NEW  alembic/versions/20260425_000001_rls_policies.py
         Postgres-only migration that calls `apply_rls_policies(bind,
         RLS_POLICIES)`. SQLite branch is a no-op (documented). Down
         calls `revert_rls_policies`.
  - NEW  tests/test_database_dialect_selection.py
         Pure-unit parametrized tests over env-var combinations:
         precedence, sslmode-require enforcement, sslmode preservation,
         per-dialect engine kwargs (SQLite / direct Postgres / pooler /
         pgbouncer query param), password stripping in
         `safe_url_for_logging`. No real DB connection.
  - NEW  tests/test_rls_policies.py
         Declarative-only: registry well-typed, expected table coverage,
         service_role-ALL invariant, validation rejects bogus
         command / empty roles / INSERT-without-WITH-CHECK,
         `apply_rls_policies` is a no-op against in-memory SQLite, and
         a pinned-DDL snapshot test that fails if `RLS_POLICIES` drifts
         from what the migration would emit.
  - NEW  docs/specs/rls_policies.md
         Why-RLS, the protected-table table, install path, why SQLite
         is a no-op, drift-detection note, and the prompt 25 follow-up
         (`founder_user_id` column).
  - NEW  .env.example
         Documents `DATABASE_URL`, `SUPABASE_DB_POOLER_URL`,
         `SUPABASE_DB_URL`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, legacy
         `COHERENCE_FUND_DATABASE_URL`, and service-identity vars.

No new runtime dependencies. SQLite path is unchanged: `python -m pytest`
and `alembic upgrade head` against the local `coherence_fund.db` continue
to work without any Supabase configuration.

                    tests/test_rls_policies.py -v -p no:pytest-qt
  PYTHONPATH=.. python3 -m alembic upgrade head    # SQLite no-op for RLS

              RLS_POLICIES, render_policy_ddl; \
              print(len(RLS_POLICIES), 'policies')"


================================================================================
  WAVE 7 — DB POOLING + READ-REPLICA + RETRY DECORATOR (prompt 23 of 70)
================================================================================

Adds (a) a configurable read-replica engine + session factory routed via
`read_only=True` flag on repositories, and (b) a transient-error retry
decorator with bounded full-jitter exponential backoff applied to the
scoring worker's job-claim and job-finish paths. SQLite default and
existing test suites are unchanged — `python -m pytest` works without
any new env vars.

  - MOD  server/fund/database.py
         Adds `resolve_replica_database_url(env)` (honors Supabase
         `sslmode=require`), `_replica_engine_kwargs_for_url(url)`
         (halves direct-Postgres `pool_size` / `max_overflow`,
         identical to primary for SQLite + pgbouncer), and
         `create_replica_engine(url)`. New `get_read_engine(env=None)`
         returns the cached replica engine when
         `SUPABASE_DB_REPLICA_URL` is set and falls back to the
         primary otherwise (test path bypasses the cache).
         New `SessionFactory(read_only=False)` is a thin callable
         that returns a session bound to either engine. New
         `retry_transient_db_errors(max_attempts=4, base_delay_ms=50,
         max_delay_ms=2000, sleeper=None, rng=None, logger=None)`
         decorator factory: full-jitter exponential backoff capped by
         `max_delay_ms`; only retries `OperationalError`,
         `DBAPIError(connection_invalidated=True)`, and Postgres
         SQLSTATEs `40001` / `40P01` / `57P01`. Never retries
         `IntegrityError` or `DataError` (logic bugs). Uses
         `secrets.SystemRandom` by default; injectable `sleeper` /
         `rng` / `logger` for deterministic tests. Emits
         `db.retry.attempt` (warning) per retry and
         `db.retry.exhausted` (error) on exhaustion.
  - MOD  server/fund/config.py
         New settings: `SUPABASE_DB_REPLICA_URL` (env
         `SUPABASE_DB_REPLICA_URL`), `DB_RETRY_MAX_ATTEMPTS`
         (env `COHERENCE_FUND_DB_RETRY_MAX_ATTEMPTS`, default 4),
         `DB_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_MS` (default 50),
         `DB_RETRY_MAX_DELAY_MS` (default 2000).
  - MOD  server/fund/repositories/__init__.py
         Now exposes `resolve_read_session(explicit, primary, *,
         read_only)` context manager: yields the explicit session if
         passed, otherwise the constructor-provided primary session,
         otherwise opens (and closes) a fresh
         `SessionFactory(read_only=...)` session for the call.
  - MOD  server/fund/repositories/portfolio_repository.py
         Read methods (`latest_state`, `active_positions_by_domain`,
         `active_positions_total`, `latest_state_as_dict`,
         `domain_concentration_by_nav`) accept keyword-only
         `session=None, read_only=False` and route through
         `resolve_read_session`. Constructor's `db` is now optional
         (`Session | None`); writes call `_require_primary()` which
         raises if no primary session was provided.
  - NEW  server/fund/repositories/applications_repository.py
         `ApplicationsReadRepository` with replica-routed reads:
         `get_application`, `get_decision`,
         `list_applications_by_founder`. Distinct from the lifecycle
         `application_repository.py` (which is write-heavy).
  - MOD  server/fund/scoring_worker.py
         New module-level `claim_next_job(repository, *, worker_id,
         lease_seconds)` and `mark_job_completed(repository, job_id)`
         decorated with `@retry_transient_db_errors(...)` from
         settings. New `_wrap_repository_with_retry(repo)` per-instance
         monkey-patches the same decorator onto
         `claim_next_scoring_job` / `mark_scoring_job_completed` so
         the service's internal job-claim and job-finish calls inherit
         the same retry budget; applied in `process_once`.
  - NEW  tests/test_db_retry_decorator.py
         18 tests. Parametrized over `SerializationFailure(40001)`,
         `DeadlockDetected(40P01)`, `OperationalError(connection_
         invalidated)`. Deterministic `_RecordingSleeper` +
         `_DeterministicRNG`. Asserts: classifier marks transients
         (incl. `57P01`); rejects `IntegrityError` / `DataError` /
         non-DBAPI errors / unknown SQLSTATE; retries-then-success
         call count + recorded delays match the predicted
         full-jitter schedule; exhaustion raises last exception and
         logs `db.retry.exhausted`; non-transient errors never sleep;
         backoff capped by `max_delay_ms`; argument validation;
         `max_attempts=1` performs no retry; decorator preserves
         `__name__` / `__doc__`.
  - NEW  tests/test_read_replica_routing.py
         15 tests. `resolve_replica_database_url` precedence
         (unset / blank / generic / Supabase / preserved sslmode).
         `get_read_engine` falls back to primary when unset, returns
         a distinct engine when set, test-path bypasses cache.
         Replica engine kwargs: half pool size for direct Postgres,
         match primary for pgbouncer / SQLite. Repository routing:
         `read_only=True` on a repository with `db=None` opens a
         session bound to the replica; with replica unset, the
         `SessionFactory(read_only=True)` session is bound to the
         primary engine.
  - NEW  docs/specs/db_pooling_and_retries.md
         Pooling table per dialect, replica SLA contract (which
         tables are safe on a replica vs. must use primary),
         transient-error classification + backoff formula, default
         retry budget table with env-var names, where the decorator
         is applied (worker job-claim/finish only — API handlers do
         NOT inherit the decorator).

No new runtime dependencies. SQLite + tests work unchanged.

================================================================================
Prompt 40 — STT abstraction (Whisper / Deepgram / AssemblyAI) with
deterministic fallback
================================================================================

Adds a SpeechToText interface plus three lazy-loaded backends behind
an STTRouter that owns provider selection, transient-failure
fallback, and the LOW_STT_CONFIDENCE quality-flag handoff to
transcript_quality. The Whisper backend never imports its native
dependency at module load — `faster_whisper` is tried first, then the
legacy `whisper` package; both missing surfaces WhisperNotAvailable
the first time `transcribe` is called.

Files:

================================================================================
PROMPT 41 — ADAPTIVE INTERVIEW POLICY ENGINE + INTERRUPTION HANDLING (Wave 11)
================================================================================

Replaces the linear topic walk in voice_intake (prompts 38–39) with
a deterministic, rules-based policy over a directed-acyclic topic
graph. After each answer the engine consults the graph + per-session
state to pick the next question — diving on weak evidence, skipping
deep follow-ups when anti-gaming flags fire, and terminating either
on coverage-met or on the per-call duration cap. Adds dropped-call
recovery with a 24h window and a hard cap of one recovery attempt
per session (state lives on InterviewSession.state_json, persisted
across reconnections).

Key invariants
  * Determinism: no LLM, no network, no clock branching in
    next_question — same (state, AnswerFeatures) → same Question.
    The fixture-walk test pins the canonical sequence
    problem → solution → evidence → moat → execution → self_critique.
  * Acyclic graph: load_topic_graph runs an iterative three-colour
    DFS and refuses cycles or unknown edge targets. Bad graphs are
    a hard load-time error, not a run-time loop.
  * Duration cap: when state.duration_seconds_used reaches
    state.duration_seconds_cap, next_question returns None and sets
    state.completed = True.
  * One recovery only: recover_session bumps state.recovery_attempts;
    a second call raises RecoveryRefused.
  * State portability: state is plain JSON (sort_keys=True), so it
    round-trips through state_json and replays without dependencies.

Files

  - NEW  server/fund/data/interview_topic_graph.json
         9 topics: problem, problem_followup, solution_mechanism,
         solution_followup, evidence, evidence_followup, moat,
         execution, self_critique. Predicates if_high_anti_gaming,
         if_low_evidence, default. high_priority_topics drive the
         coverage criterion. duration_seconds_cap=1800,
         confidence_threshold=0.6, anti_gaming_threshold=1,
         max_follow_ups_per_topic=1.
  - NEW  server/fund/services/interview_policy.py
         TopicGraph / TopicNode / Question / AnswerFeatures
         dataclasses; load_topic_graph (cycle + reachability
         validation); init_state; apply_answer; next_question;
         coverage_complete; duration_exhausted; deterministic edge
         selection with fixed predicate priority (anti_gaming >
         low_evidence > default).
  - NEW  server/fund/services/interview_recovery.py
         should_recover predicate (status check, completion check,
         coverage check, recovery_attempts cap, 24h window);
         recover_session (notifier + redialer callables injected
         for testability); resume_question helper; RecoveryRefused
         for already-attempted / window-expired / no-next-question.
  - NEW  alembic/versions/20260425_000008_interview_session_state.py
         add fund_interview_sessions.state_json TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT
         '' (empty == no policy state yet; policy initialises lazily).
  - MOD  server/fund/models.py
         InterviewSession.state_json: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(
             Text, nullable=False, default="", server_default="")
  - MOD  server/fund/services/voice_intake.py
         start_call seeds state_json with init_state on session
         creation. New helper next_question_for_session(db, session,
         features=None) loads/runs/saves state via the policy
         engine. Existing TwiML render functions are unchanged so
         the pinned snapshot test in test_voice_intake.py still
         passes.
  - NEW  tests/test_interview_policy.py (13 tests)
         load + acyclic check; cycle rejection; unknown-edge
         rejection; init_state semantics; first-call returns start;
         high-evidence walk skips followups; low-evidence routes
         to follow-up + max_follow_ups guard; anti-gaming overrides
         low-evidence; duration cap terminates; coverage_complete
         terminates; determinism; full canonical walk; follow-up
         counter increment.
  - NEW  tests/test_interview_recovery.py (8 tests)
         should_recover true / false-when-completed / false-out-of-
         window; resume from next_question; refuses second attempt;
         refuses when no next_question; resume_question round-trip;
         works without notifier/redialer.
  - NEW  docs/specs/interview_policy.md
         Goals, components, topic graph format, predicate priority
         rules, coverage criterion, session-state schema, 24h
         recovery flow, determinism + replay guarantees.

Verification:
  python3 -m pytest tests/test_interview_policy.py \
                    tests/test_interview_recovery.py -v \
                    -p no:pytest-qt -p no:pytestqt
    # 21 passed
  python3 -m pytest tests/test_voice_intake.py -v \
                    -p no:pytest-qt -p no:pytestqt
    # 8 passed (no regression in pinned TwiML snapshot or
    #           existing voice-intake lifecycle tests)
  python3 -m pytest tests/ -q -p no:pytest-qt -p no:pytestqt \

    # 1055 passed; pre-existing failures only (worker_backend_switch

PROMPT 42 — HISTORICAL-STARTUPS VALIDATION CORPUS SCHEMA + INGESTION HARNESS
  Goal: stand up the data layer for the predictive-validity study (500 rows

PROMPT 44 — COHERENCE-VS-OUTCOME REGRESSION STUDY WITH BOOTSTRAPPED CIs
  Goal: deterministic, replayable predictive-validity harness that joins
  the historical-pitch corpus with realized outcomes, fits
  ``logit(survival_5yr) ~ coherence_score + domain_primary +
  log(check_size_usd)``, and emits a pre-registered report with
  bootstrap CIs, Brier, AUC, calibration curve, and per-domain
  sub-models — refusing to run when N(known outcome) < 200.

  - NEW  data/governed/validation/preregistration.yaml
         Frozen study contract. Primary hypothesis H1 (coherence_score
         positively associated with survival_5yr at α=0.01), secondary
         hypothesis H2 (monotonic non-decreasing dose-response across
         coherence quintiles, Q5 - Q1 ≥ 0.05), Bonferroni correction
         across per-domain sub-models, n=10000 stdlib-RNG bootstrap,
         minimum_n_with_known_outcome=200, negative-results-publishing
         policy, and an explicit prediction-not-causation scope
         boundary. Bumping any field requires a new ``version:`` plus
         an ``amendments:`` entry; the loader rejects documents with
         missing required keys.
  - NEW  server/fund/services/validation_study.py
         StudyConfig / StudyRow / StudyReport dataclasses; pure-stdlib
         logistic regression via Newton-Raphson IRLS with a tiny ridge
         (1e-6) for stability; deterministic row-level bootstrap via
         random.Random(seed); _percentile() linear-interpolation
         percentile; brier_score / auc_roc (Mann-Whitney with average
         ranks for ties) / calibration_curve (10 equal-width bins);
         _evaluate_primary (rejects H0 when 1-α CI excludes 0 *and*
         direction matches); _evaluate_quintile_dose_response (5
         equal-count rank-quintiles); _per_domain_models (Bonferroni-
         corrected sub-models for domains with N≥30; smaller domains
         are reported in insufficient_subgroups); _detect_optional_libs
         records numpy/statsmodels/sklearn versions in generated_with
         purely for audit (math is stdlib regardless of availability);
         a tiny stdlib YAML reader for the preregistration document
         (no PyYAML runtime dependency); InsufficientSampleError when
         N < pre-registered minimum.
  - NEW  server/fund/services/validation_report.py
         render_markdown(report_dict) → Markdown brief mentioning N,
         primary/secondary decisions, AUC/Brier, the calibration table,
         the coefficient table with 95/99 % CIs, per-domain sub-models
         with Bonferroni-corrected CIs, and the disclosure section
         (claim_kind=prediction). Pure function of the report payload;
         deterministic.
  - MOD  cli.py
         Adds ``validation-study run --output ... [--seed N
         --manifest ... --outcomes ... --scores ... --preregistration
         ... --bootstrap-iters N]`` and ``validation-study report --in
         <report.json>``. run exits 2 with INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE if the
         joined frame is too small. report renders the canonical JSON
         to Markdown.
  - NEW  deploy/scripts/run_validation_study.py
         Operator entry point (same flags as the CLI verb) for
         ops-context invocations without an editable install. Exits 0
         on success, 2 on validation-study errors.
  - NEW  tests/test_validation_study.py — 14 tests, all pass:
         * Brier perfect/worst, AUC perfect/all-tied, calibration
           bin-count sanity.
         * fit_logit recovers the sign on a clean simulated dataset.
         * load_preregistration loads the on-disk YAML; missing-key
           preregistration raises PreregistrationError.
         * Stopping rule: N=50 raises InsufficientSampleError carrying
           the operator-greppable INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE token.
         * Determinism: same (seed, output_path, frame) → same digest
           and byte-identical artifact across two runs of run_study;
           different output_path is the only allowed source of
           divergence.
         * Different bootstrap seeds → different CIs but identical
           point estimates.
         * Power: 3 (data_seed, boot_seed) parameterizations on a
           400-row planted-effect frame all recover sign and reject H0
           at the pre-registered α=0.01.
         * Quintile dose-response is monotonic on the planted frame.
         * Markdown renderer mentions headline facts.
  - NEW  docs/specs/validation_study.md
         Pre-registration policy, report shape, determinism contract,
         negative-results commitment, prediction-not-causation
         boundary, runbooks for ``validation-study run|report`` and
         ``deploy/scripts/run_validation_study.py``, glossary for
         Brier / AUC / calibration.

Verification:

                    -p no:pytest-qt

                    --output /tmp/study.json

    # operator backfills outcome rows + a scores artifact before the

Prompt 44 prohibitions honored:
  * Pre-registration document is loaded into every report; bumping any
    pinned constant requires a ``version:`` change + an ``amendments:``

    data is touched.

PROMPT 45 — LEAKAGE AUDIT + TEMPORAL PRE/POST-2020 HOLDOUT SPLITTER
  Goal: a mandatory, hard-failing audit pass that runs *before* any
  validation-study report is rendered. Verifies (a) no holdout pitch
  was used to fit any embedding / anti-gaming / contradiction-direction
  artifact, (b) the corpus splits cleanly across the pre/post-2020
  buffer year, and (c) per-feature training/holdout marginals do not
  drift. Failures raise LEAKAGE_DETECTED and block publication.

  - NEW  server/fund/services/temporal_split.py
         SplitConfig / SplitResult / pitch_year_of / split. Pinned
         defaults (train_end="2019-12-31", buffer_year=2020,
         holdout_start="2021-01-01"). Pitches dated within the buffer
         year are placed in SplitResult.buffer_excluded and never reach
         either partition. Undated rows are sequestered in
         undated_excluded so the caller can see them. SplitConfig
         rejects an inverted window at construction time.
  - NEW  server/fund/services/leakage_audit.py
         AuditConfig / LeakageReport / FeatureDriftResult /
         ArtifactMembershipResult / TemporalSplitSummary dataclasses;
         load_training_artifacts_index (JSON loader + schema check);
         ks_two_sample (pure-stdlib two-sample KS with tie handling +
         alpha=0.05 critical 1.36 / sqrt((n1+n2)/(n1*n2)));
         population_stability_index (training-quantile bins, ε-floored
         log term); thresholds PSI ≥ 0.25 → warn, ≥ 0.50 → error;
         audit() composes the three checks (membership, temporal split,
         drift) into a structured report and computes a stable
         audit_digest; enforce() raises LeakageDetectedError (code =
         "LEAKAGE_DETECTED") on any failed assertion. Buffer override
         requires an explicit buffer_override_rationale.
  - NEW  data/governed/training_artifacts_index.json
         Schema training-artifacts-index-v1. Three artifacts seeded
         (contradiction_direction_c_hat, anti_gaming_template_set,
         calibration_curve_v1) each with empty training_pitch_ids and
         training_set_hash="PENDING_FIRST_FIT" (filled in by the
         operator at first fit). The audit warns if a declared
         training_set_hash diverges from the recomputed sha256 over
         sorted training_pitch_ids.
  - MOD  server/fund/services/validation_study.py
         StudyConfig adds training_artifacts_index_path and
         audit_feature_extractors. run_study runs the leakage audit
         after fit/metric computation and BEFORE writing the canonical
         bytes; a failed audit raises LeakageDetectedError and no
         output is produced. generated_with records
         leakage_audit_digest + leakage_audit_passed.
  - MOD  cli.py
         New ``leakage audit`` verb with --manifest /
         --training-artifacts-index / --feature (repeatable) /
         --train-end / --buffer-year / --holdout-start /
         --buffer-override-rationale / --output flags. Exit 0 on pass,
         2 on LEAKAGE_DETECTED.
  - NEW  tests/test_leakage_audit.py — 15 tests, all pass:
         * temporal_split: buffer-year exclusion, inverted-window
           rejection, undated-row sequestration.
         * artifact membership: planted overlap is detected and
           LeakageDetectedError carries the LEAKAGE_DETECTED code.
         * clean case passes; PSI / KS sanity (zero on identical,
           alarm on disjoint) for pure-stdlib stats.
         * distribution drift: planted shift trips PSI ≥ 0.50 error
           band and the audit fails.
         * buffer override without rationale fails; with rationale
           passes.
         * declared holdout outside the post-buffer window flagged.
         * Validation-study integration: planted-leak corpus causes
           run_study to raise LeakageDetectedError BEFORE any output
           bytes are written (the output file does not exist after
           the failed call).
  - NEW  docs/specs/leakage_audit.md
         Buffer-year rationale, three-assertion contract,
         training-artifacts-index protocol, operator runbook,
         determinism guarantees, prompt-45 prohibitions.

Verification:
  /usr/local/bin/python3 -m pytest tests/test_leakage_audit.py \
                    tests/test_validation_study.py -v -p no:pytest-qt
    # 29 passed in ~20s
  PYTHONPATH=.. python3 -m coherence_engine leakage audit
    # passed=true, n_train=18, n_holdout=2, n_buffer_excluded=5
    # against the on-disk historical_corpus manifest.

Prompt 45 prohibitions honored:
  * Leakage audit on study render is mandatory; no bypass flag exists.
    run_study calls leakage_audit.audit + leakage_audit.enforce before
    writing any canonical bytes. Tested via
    test_validation_study_blocks_render_on_leakage.
  * Buffer year defaults to 2020 and shrinking it requires an explicit
    --buffer-year override + a non-empty buffer_override_rationale.
    Tested via test_audit_rejects_buffer_override_without_rationale.
  * The holdout set is derived from the temporal split of the corpus,
    NOT from any artifact's training pool — the audit explicitly
    checks the inverse direction (holdout ∩ training_pitch_ids must
    be empty per artifact).
  * No edits outside SCOPE.

PROMPT 47 — Cosine Paradox replication harness (Wave 13)
================================================================

Independent replication of the Cosine Paradox claim
(`apps/site/.../research/cosine_paradox.mdx`). The headline tested
is the stronger working interpretation: that *entailment and
contradiction NLI pairs are statistically indistinguishable in raw
all-mpnet-base-v2 cosine space*. Replication targets SNLI dev
(MultiNLI matched fallback) — never the encoder's training corpus.

NEW  Experiments/__init__.py
NEW  Experiments/Cosine_Paradox_Replication/__init__.py
NEW  Experiments/Cosine_Paradox_Replication/preregistration.yaml
       Frozen study parameters: alpha=0.01, n_permutations=10000,
       n_bootstrap=10000, seed=47, stopping_rule.minimum_n_per_label
       =200. Embedder pinned to sentence-transformers/all-mpnet-
       base-v2. Leakage assumption documented (SNLI/MultiNLI are
       *plausibly* in all-mpnet-base-v2 pre-training mix; empirical
       overlap check not performed; flagged in every report).
       Prohibitions: no fine-tuning on replication data, no post-hoc
       alpha/test-statistic adjustment, no metric swap, no label
       discard.
NEW  Experiments/Cosine_Paradox_Replication/run_replication.py
       Stdlib-only deterministic harness. Mann-Whitney U with
       average-rank tie correction; rank-biserial effect size
       r = 2*U_a/(n1*n2) - 1 (Wendt); 95% bootstrap CI on r via
       stratified resample with stdlib random.Random(seed); two-
       sided permutation p-value with additive smoothing
       (count+1)/(iters+1). Cosines may come from a precomputed
       JSON, a labeled NLI .jsonl + production embedder, or the
       bundled fixture (dry-run + tests). Refuses network unless
       --allow-network. Refuses to emit when any label group <
       minimum_n_per_label, except when source=="fixture".
       Falsification rule pinned in module: |r| >= 0.20 AND
       p < 0.01 -> paradox_refuted; otherwise paradox_confirmed.
       Canonical JSON report (sorted keys, 10-digit-rounded floats)
       is byte-identical across runs; run_id derives from
       sha256(cosines_digest|seed|iters|alpha)[:16].
NEW  Experiments/Cosine_Paradox_Replication/expected_report.json
       Pinned baseline produced by `--dry-run` against the bundled
       tiny fixture. Test suite asserts byte-identical match (after
       stripping the volatile `generated_with` block which records
       detected library versions).
NEW  Experiments/Cosine_Paradox_Replication/fixtures/
       tiny_nli_fixture.json — 24 hand-picked cosines (8 per label)
       designed so entailment/contradiction overlap (paradox
       confirmed: r=0.1875, p=0.5335) and neutral is clearly
       separable from both (r=-1.0, p=0.001).
MOD  cli.py
       New `replication cosine-paradox` verb with --dry-run /
       --cosines / --dataset / --output / --seed /
       --n-permutations / --n-bootstrap-iterations /
       --allow-network / --preregistration /
       --minimum-n-per-label flags. Exit 0 on success, 2 on
       missing args, 3 on INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE.
NEW  tests/test_cosine_paradox_replication.py — 18 tests, all pass:
       * statistical primitives: ranks-with-ties, Mann-Whitney U
         on perfectly-separated groups, rank-biserial bounds at
         {-1, 0, +1}, descriptive stats sanity, permutation p
         low on separable / high on overlapping groups.
       * preregistration loads with required keys and matches the
         pinned values (seed=47, alpha=0.01, n_perm=10000,
         min_n=200).
       * end-to-end: dry-run output matches expected_report.json
         numerically to 1e-6, byte-identical across two consecutive
         runs, paradox_confirmed on the fixture, secondary tests
         (neutral-vs-{ent,con}) reject H0 with |r| >= 0.95.
       * inputs.cosines_digest_sha256 changes when fixture cosines
         change.
       * changing seed changes bootstrap CI but never the
         deterministic Mann-Whitney U or rank-biserial point.
       * INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE raised when source != "fixture" and
         any group is below minimum_n_per_label.
       * --dataset without --allow-network refused
         (NetworkAccessDenied).
       * Falsification threshold pinned at 0.20 (regression test
         against post-hoc loosening).
       * CLI smoke: subprocess-launched dry-run produces report
         that matches expected_report.json numerically.
NEW  docs/research/cosine_paradox_replication.md
       Design table (replication vs. original paper), falsification
       criterion stated word-for-word, operating procedure, full
       determinism contract, statistical methods (stdlib, no
       scipy), leakage caveat, file index, out-of-scope.

Verification:
  arch -arm64 python3 -m pytest \
    tests/test_cosine_paradox_replication.py -v
    # 18 passed in ~5s
  arch -arm64 python3 -m coherence_engine replication \
    cosine-paradox --dry-run
    # emits canonical JSON to stdout; byte-identical to the
    # pinned expected_report.json (modulo generated_with).

Prompt 47 prohibitions honored:
  * The harness has NO fine-tuning code path. The embedder is
    pulled via the production `get_embedder()` factory; its weights
    are not touched, and the prereg's prohibited_actions list has
    "tuning the embedder on the replication dataset" first.
  * The falsification threshold (0.20) is pinned both in
    preregistration.yaml AND in run_replication._FALSIFICATION_-
    EFFECT_THRESHOLD; alpha is in preregistration.yaml. Both are
    asserted in tests.
  * Leakage assumption documented in preregistration.yaml under
    `leakage_assumption.text`, the harness echoes it into every
    emitted report, and the doc spells out that this is a
    replication on plausibly-overlapping data — strengthening
    requires re-running on a corpus published *after* the
    encoder's snapshot date.
  * No edits outside SCOPE.

PROMPT 48 — Contradiction-direction (ĉ) cross-domain stability (Wave 13)
================================================================

Cross-domain stability study for the contradiction-direction vector
ĉ derived in apps/site/src/content/research/contradiction_direction.mdx.
Tests whether a single global ĉ generalises across MultiNLI genre
domains, or whether the engine must carry one fitted ĉ per domain.

NEW  core/contradiction_direction.py
       Production surface for ĉ. `fit_c_hat(pairs) -> np.ndarray`
       computes per-pair Householder normals
       n_i = (u_i - v_i) / ||u_i - v_i||, then takes the leading
       right singular vector of the stacked normals as the principal
       contradiction axis. Sign is canonicalised so the first non-
       zero coordinate is positive — two runs produce byte-identical
       ĉ. Companion functions: `pair_directions`, `project` (the
       sign-invariant |⟨u-v, ĉ⟩| score used for ROC), `cosine`,
       `abs_cosine` (sign-invariant cosine — the right metric for
       comparing ĉ vectors).
NEW  Experiments/Contradiction_Direction_Stability/__init__.py
NEW  Experiments/Contradiction_Direction_Stability/preregistration.yaml
       Frozen study parameters: n_subsamples=50, subsample_sizes=
       {200, 500, 1000}, bootstrap iterations=1000, seeds split into
       per_domain_fit / cross_domain_eval / subsample_master /
       bootstrap_master, stopping_rule.minimum_pairs_per_domain_label
       =200. Domains drawn from MultiNLI matched-dev `genre` field
       (fiction, government, slate, telephone, travel). Decision rule
       (H1): single ĉ holds when pairwise abs-cosine min >= 0.70 AND
       median cross-domain AUC drop <= 0.05. Cross-fit protocol
       pinned in prereg: ĉ fit on A is evaluated only on held-out B
       pairs; within-domain baseline uses a deterministic 50/50 split.
       Prohibitions: no in-sample AUC reporting, no post-hoc
       threshold relaxation, no domain-averaging before reporting,
       no metric swap.
NEW  Experiments/Contradiction_Direction_Stability/run_stability_study.py
       Numpy + stdlib deterministic harness, sharing the YAML parser,
       rank-with-ties, percentile, optional-package detector, and
       round-floats helpers from the cosine-paradox harness so the two
       studies emit reports under one contract. Reports five blocks:
       per_domain_c_hat, pairwise_cosine (full N×N abs-cosine matrix
       with 95% bootstrap CIs), cross_domain_auc (within-domain
       baseline + full cross-domain matrix annotated with
       auc_drop_vs_baseline), subsample_sensitivity (mean/std/CI of
       abs-cosine to ĉ(full pool) at each pre-registered N), and
       decision (criterion text, thresholds, observed quantities,
       boolean single_c_hat_holds, outcome string). Falsification
       thresholds pinned in module:
       _FALSIFICATION_PAIRWISE_COSINE = 0.70 and
       _FALSIFICATION_AUC_DROP = 0.05. ROC AUC computed via the rank-
       sum formula with average-rank tie correction. Bootstrap CIs
       use stdlib random.Random for index sampling so byte-identity
       does not depend on numpy.random version drift.
NEW  Experiments/Contradiction_Direction_Stability/fixtures/
       tiny_two_domain_fixture.json — 2 synthetic domains, 16
       contradiction + 16 entailment pairs each, dim=4. Domain A's
       contradiction axis is e_0; domain B's is e_1 — orthogonal by
       construction. End-to-end the harness recovers ĉ_a ≈ e_0,
       ĉ_b ≈ e_1, pairwise abs-cosine ≈ 0, within-domain AUC = 1.0,
       cross-domain AUC = 0.0, decision = per_domain_c_hat_required.
       The harness skips stopping_rule when source=="fixture" so
       dry-run + tests can run on n=16.
MOD  cli.py
       New `replication c-hat-stability` verb with --dry-run /
       --corpus / --output / --seed / --n-bootstrap-iterations /
       --n-subsamples / --preregistration /
       --minimum-pairs-per-domain-label flags. Refactored
       `_cmd_replication` to dispatch between `cosine-paradox` and
       `c-hat-stability` subcommands. Exit 0 on success, 2 on
       missing args, 3 on INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE.
NEW  tests/test_c_hat_stability.py — 19 tests, all pass:
       * fit_c_hat geometry: single-pair Householder normal, sign
         canonicalisation, principal-axis recovery on a 20-pair
         e_1-aligned set with 2 e_2-aligned outliers, normalised
         pair_directions, sign-invariant abs_cosine, sign-dropping
         project, error-on-empty / error-on-wrong-shape.
       * Synthetic 2-domain fixture: orthogonal ĉ recovered (abs-
         cosine < 0.30), within-domain AUC > 0.85, cross-domain AUC
         < 0.70, decision = per_domain_c_hat_required, subsample
         sensitivity reports each pre-registered N.
       * Determinism: two consecutive runs produce byte-identical
         canonical bytes (modulo `generated_with`); same seed produces
         the same run_id; different seed changes bootstrap CIs but
         not per-domain ĉ vectors or pairwise abs-cosine point
         estimates (those are seed-free by SVD).
       * Preregistration: loads from disk with required keys, missing
         corpus + fixture path raises StabilityError.
       * CLI smoke: subprocess-launched dry-run produces report with
         expected schema_version and decision outcome.
NEW  docs/research/contradiction_direction_stability.md
       Operationalisation table, decision rule stated word-for-word
       with both thresholds, cross-fit protocol (no leakage),
       determinism contract mirroring cosine-paradox, operating
       procedure with corpus JSON shape, synthetic-fixture sanity
       check description, report-block walkthrough, limits, and
       file index.

Verification:

PROMPT 49 — Hoyer-sparsity vs raw-cosine head-to-head ROC (Wave 13)
================================================================

Head-to-head ROC comparison of three discriminators of NLI
contradiction vs entailment: raw cosine, Hoyer-sparsity of the
difference vector (u - v), and ĉ-projection |⟨u-v, ĉ⟩|. Tests the
Guide-3 claim that the engine's signal is *meaningfully different*
from raw cosine. The DeLong two-sided z-test is the load-bearing
inferential statistic for the AUC comparison.

NEW  Experiments/Hoyer_vs_Cosine/__init__.py
NEW  Experiments/Hoyer_vs_Cosine/preregistration.yaml
       Frozen study parameters: alpha=0.01, n_bootstrap=10000,
       random_seed=49, minimum_eval_pairs_per_label=200 (post 50/50
       split, so corpus must carry ≥400 per label), encoder pinned
       to sentence-transformers/all-mpnet-base-v2, neutral excluded
       from binary task. Decision rule (H1): DeLong two-sided
       p-value < alpha rejects equality of AUCs; direction read off
       sign of auc_diff. Cross-fit protocol: ĉ fit on fit-half of
       contradiction pairs ONLY; all three scores evaluated on
       eval-halves of both labels (paired). directionality_note
       explicitly justifies the two-sided test (Guide-3 claim is
       "different", not "better"; one-sided would let cosine-wins
       slip past the gate). Prohibitions: no in-sample evaluation
       of ĉ, no unpaired AUC comparison, no post-hoc one-sided
       switch, no AUC point estimates without CIs, no eval-pair
       discards, no encoder tuning.
NEW  Experiments/Hoyer_vs_Cosine/run_comparison.py
       Numpy + stdlib deterministic harness reusing the cosine-
       paradox YAML parser, ranks-with-ties, percentile, optional-
       package detector, and round-floats helpers so all three
       Wave-13 studies emit reports under one contract. Implements
       DeLong directly (no scipy dependency): psi(a,b) matrix,
       V10 / V01 placement values, sample covariance via centered
       outer product, and z = (AUC_a - AUC_b) /
       sqrt(S[a,a] + S[b,b] - 2*S[a,b]) with two-sided p via the
       erf normal CDF. Three score functions: cosine = 1 - cos(u,v),
       hoyer = hoyer_sparsity(u-v), projection = |⟨u-v, ĉ⟩|. Paired
       bootstrap CI samples one set of indices per iteration and
       computes all three AUCs on it. Reports four blocks: auc
       (point + CI per classifier), delong (hoyer_vs_cosine +
       projection_vs_cosine, each with auc_diff, var_diff, z,
       p_value, reject_null, winner ∈ {hoyer | projection | cosine
       | no_difference}, null_hypothesis), interpretation
       (primary_outcome, primary_winner, criterion, directionality),
       and inputs (digest, n_pairs total/fit/eval, c_hat_norm,
       minimum_eval_pairs).
NEW  Experiments/Hoyer_vs_Cosine/fixtures/tiny_pair_fixture.json
       24 contradiction + 24 entailment pairs in dim=8. Both
       labels' difference vectors are constructed orthogonal to u
       with matching magnitudes so cosine(u,v) overlaps heavily
       across labels (cos AUC ≈ 0.5); entailment deltas are dense
       (uniform direction → low Hoyer), contradiction deltas are
       single-axis impulses (perfect Hoyer = 1.0). Hoyer dominates
       cosine *by construction*. Stopping rule skipped on
       source=="fixture".
MOD  cli.py
       New `replication hoyer-vs-cosine` verb with --dry-run /
       --corpus / --output / --seed / --n-bootstrap-iterations /
       --preregistration / --minimum-eval-pairs-per-label flags.
       `_cmd_replication` extended to dispatch among cosine-paradox
       | c-hat-stability | hoyer-vs-cosine. Exit 0 success, 2
       missing args, 3 INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE.
NEW  tests/test_hoyer_vs_cosine.py — 20 tests, all pass:
       * ROC AUC primitives: perfect separation = 1.0, inverted =
         0.0, all-ties = 0.5, empty class = 0.5.
       * DeLong: identical classifiers → var_diff=0 + p=1; synthetic
         where Hoyer cleanly separates and cosine is noise →
         rejects at p < 0.01; unequal-length inputs raise
         ValueError; two-sided p is symmetric in argument ordering.
       * Pre-registration loads with required keys; pinned alpha,
         n_bootstrap, seed, minimum_eval_pairs match expected;
         primary_hypothesis test field contains "two-sided".
       * End-to-end on fixture: AUC(hoyer) ≥ 0.95, AUC(cosine) ≈
         0.5, DeLong rejects equality, primary_outcome =
         "hoyer_signal_differs_from_cosine", winner = "hoyer";
         projection also beats cosine.
       * Determinism: byte-identical canonical bytes across runs;
         changing seed changes CIs (and the eval split); inputs
         digest sensitive to single-coord perturbation.
       * Stopping rule raises InsufficientEvalSampleError on a
         non-fixture corpus below the minimum; missing fixture +
         corpus path raises ComparisonError.
       * Report has all required blocks; every AUC point estimate
         carries its CI (the prohibition guard); schema_version
         pinned at "hoyer-vs-cosine-v1".
       * CLI smoke via subprocess: dry-run produces report with
         expected schema_version and primary_outcome.
NEW  docs/research/hoyer_vs_cosine.md
       Operationalisation table, falsification criterion stated
       word-for-word with two-sided justification, DeLong walk-
       through (psi matrix, V10/V01 placement values, sandwich
       variance, why paired beats unpaired), cross-fit protocol,
       determinism contract mirroring the other Wave-13 studies,
       operating procedure with corpus JSON shape, synthetic-fixture
       sanity check with the expected numbers, report-block
       walkthrough, limits, file index.

PROMPT 50 — Reverse-Marxism reflection-recovery rigor (Wave 13)
================================================================

Replicates the headline 84.3% Householder-reflection recovery
claim (apps/site/.../research/reverse_marxism.mdx) under stricter
conditions. The original number was reported on the same Marx
text used to fit the class axis. This study tests whether the
recovery property survives:

  (a) held-out concept axes — axis fit on training slab, recovery
      evaluated on a non-overlapping held-out slab of labeled
      sentences;
  (b) bootstrapped CI on the held-out recovery rate (10 000
      iterations, 95% by default);
  (c) random-reflection null baseline — 100 random unit vectors
      as reflection axes, recovery rate per axis, empirical CI
      across the null distribution;
  (d) pre-registered alpha sensitivity sweep over the frozen grid
      {0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0, 2.5, 3.0}.

Decision rule (H1): the headline 84.3% generalises when the held-
out recovery's lower 95% CI at alpha=2 exceeds the random-baseline
upper 95% CI at alpha=2. Both outcomes are publishable per the
negative-results policy; refutation is the load-bearing finding.

NEW  Experiments/Reverse_Marxism_Rigor/__init__.py
NEW  Experiments/Reverse_Marxism_Rigor/preregistration.yaml
       Frozen study parameters: random_seed=50, n_random_axes=100,
       n_bootstrap=10000, ci_percent=95.0, alpha_grid=[0.5, 1.0,
       1.5, 2.0, 2.5, 3.0], minimum_holdout_sentences=50,
       minimum_axis_seeds=5. Encoder pinned to sentence-
       transformers/all-mpnet-base-v2. Axis construction:
       centroid-of-seed-embeddings then L2-normalise. Reflection
       formula: v_prime = v - alpha*dot(v, axis)*axis. Held-out
       protocol forbids axis fit on holdout sentences and
       evaluation on training sentences (HeldOutLeakageError).
       Random-baseline rule reports empirical CI across n random
       axes per alpha; the 0.5 idealised null is documented but
       NOT used as the decision threshold. prohibited_actions:
       fitting axis on evaluation corpus, single point estimate
       without null comparison, post-hoc alpha selection, holdout
       discards after seeing scores, operationalisation swap,
       seed amendment without version bump.
NEW  Experiments/Reverse_Marxism_Rigor/run_rigor_study.py
       Numpy + stdlib deterministic harness reusing the cosine-
       paradox YAML parser, percentile, optional-package
       detector, and round-floats helpers so all four Wave-13
       studies emit reports under one contract. Implements the
       generalised Householder reflection v - alpha*(v.a)*a, axis
       fit via centroid-then-L2-normalise, sign-on-axis recovery
       operationalisation, random unit-vector sampling
       (Gaussian-then-L2-normalise), bootstrap CI on the recovery
       rate via stdlib random.Random, and the per-alpha random-
       axis null distribution summary. Decision block reports
       primary_held_out_ci_low, primary_random_baseline_ci_high,
       primary_margin, primary_generalises, primary_outcome
       (reflection_recovery_generalises_held_out |
        reflection_recovery_does_not_generalise_held_out), plus a
       secondary_pass on alpha=2 vs max(alpha=0.5, 1.0) using the
       baseline std as threshold. Alpha keys are canonicalised in
       the report as f"alpha_{value:.4f}" so the bytes do not
       depend on float formatting.
NEW  Experiments/Reverse_Marxism_Rigor/fixtures/tiny_rigor_fixture.json
       8 axis seeds clustered along e_0 + 60 holdout sentences in
       dim=16 (30 with positive projection on e_0 and label=+1,
       30 with negative projection and label=-1). Recovery is
       perfect at alpha>=1.5; random-axis baseline is well below
       the held-out CI by construction (random unit vectors hardly
       perturb the projection on the fitted axis in 16 dimensions).
       Stopping rule skipped on source=="fixture".
MOD  cli.py
       New `replication reverse-marxism-rigor` verb with --dry-run /
       --corpus / --output / --seed / --n-bootstrap / --n-random-
       axes / --preregistration / --minimum-holdout-sentences /
       --minimum-axis-seeds flags. `_cmd_replication` extended to
       dispatch among cosine-paradox | c-hat-stability | hoyer-vs-
       cosine | reverse-marxism-rigor. Exit 0 success, 2 missing
       args, 3 INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLE.
NEW  tests/test_reverse_marxism_rigor.py — 28 tests, all pass:
       * Reflection math: alpha=2 flips axis projection sign while
         leaving orthogonal components unchanged; alpha=1 zeroes
         the axis projection; alpha=0 is identity.
       * Axis fit: centroid-then-normalise; zero-centroid raises.
       * Recovery rate: perfect axis -> perfect recovery; reflect
         axis orthogonal to eval axis -> 0 recovery (no flip).
       * Random unit vector sampling: shape and unit norm.
       * Bootstrap CI: all-successes -> [1, 1]; all-failures ->
         [0, 0]; balanced inputs -> mean near 0.5 with non-zero std.
       * Pre-registration loads with required keys; pinned seed,
         n_bootstrap, n_random_axes, alpha_grid, minimum_holdout
         match expected; alpha=2 in grid; held_out_protocol +
         random_baseline blocks present; prohibited_actions covers
         "post-hoc alpha" and "single point estimate".
       * End-to-end on fixture: held-out recovery at alpha=2 >=
         0.95, random-baseline mean far below 0.5, held-out CI low
         > baseline CI high; decision.primary_generalises = true,
         primary_outcome = reflection_recovery_generalises_held_out,
         primary_margin > 0; alpha sweep includes the full grid.
       * Determinism: byte-identical canonical bytes across runs;
         changing seed alters baseline but not the fitted axis;
         inputs digest sensitive to a single-coord perturbation.
       * Held-out leakage detected: a holdout sentence equal to an
         axis seed raises HeldOutLeakageError before any output.
       * Stopping rule raises InsufficientHoldoutError on a
         non-fixture corpus below the minimum; missing fixture +
         corpus path raises RigorError; invalid ideology_label
         (anything outside {-1, +1}) raises RigorError.
       * Report has all required blocks; every alpha carries
         {ci_low, ci_high, ci_percent} on both held_out_recovery
         and random_baseline (the no-point-estimate-without-CI
         guard); schema_version pinned at "reverse-marxism-rigor-v1".
       * Decision uses the empirical baseline CI, NOT the 0.5
         idealisation — that delegation is the rigor study's
         value-add.
       * CLI smoke via subprocess: dry-run produces report with
         expected schema_version, headline_alpha=2.0, and
         primary_outcome.
NEW  docs/research/reverse_marxism_rigor.md
       Operationalisation table (axis fit, generalised reflection,
       label semantics, recovery success, baseline construction),
       falsification criterion stated word-for-word with the
       empirical-baseline rationale, held-out and random-baseline
       protocol notes, determinism contract mirroring the other
       Wave-13 studies, operating procedure with corpus JSON shape,
       synthetic-fixture sanity check with the expected numbers,
       limits, file index.

    # "reflection_recovery_generalises_held_out", held-out

Prompt 50 prohibitions honored:
  * Held-out protocol enforced. The harness raises
    HeldOutLeakageError if any axis seed appears verbatim (1e-8
    precision) in the holdout slab. Pre-registration's
    held_out_protocol section forbids fitting on evaluation data;
    test_held_out_leakage_detected exercises the guard.
  * Random-reflection null comparison is mandatory. The decision
    block requires both primary_held_out_ci_low and
    primary_random_baseline_ci_high; the harness reports a per-
    alpha random-baseline distribution and uses its empirical CI
    high as the threshold. test_decision_uses_empirical_baseline_
    not_idealised_05 enforces that the 0.5 idealisation is NOT
    the decision threshold.
  * Alpha grid is frozen in preregistration.yaml and parsed up
    front; the harness runs every value in the grid and reports
    them all. prohibited_actions explicitly forbids post-hoc alpha
    selection. test_dry_run_alpha_sweep_includes_full_grid asserts
    the full grid {0.5, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0, 2.5, 3.0} is present.
  * No edits outside SCOPE. Files modified: cli.py,
    COHERENCE_ENGINE_PROJECT_STATUS.txt,

    four Experiments/Reverse_Marxism_Rigor/* artifacts,
    tests/test_reverse_marxism_rigor.py,
    docs/research/reverse_marxism_rigor.md.

PROMPT 51 — STRIPE CONNECT + BANK-TRANSFER ADAPTER FOR CAPITAL DEPLOYMENT
  Goal: a CapitalDeployment surface that prepares investment-transfer
  instructions and routes them through pluggable backends (Stripe
  Connect for non-US founder payouts; BankTransfer / Mercury for
  ACH/wire) without ever moving money autonomously. The system
  prepares; an authenticated `treasurer` approves; a `treasurer`
  executes. Dual approval is required for amounts ≥ $250k.

  - NEW  alembic/versions/20260425_000009_capital_deployment.py
         fund_investment_instructions (id, application_id, founder_id,
         amount_usd, currency, target_account_ref, preparation_method,
         status, provider_intent_ref, idempotency_key, prepared_by,
         treasurer_id, error_code, prepared_at, approved_at, sent_at)
         + fund_treasurer_approvals (id, instruction_id, treasurer_id,
         decision, note, created_at) with a unique index on
         (instruction_id, treasurer_id) so the same human cannot
         double-sign to satisfy dual approval.
  - MOD  server/fund/models.py
         InvestmentInstruction + TreasurerApproval ORM rows backing
         the migration. ``approvals`` relationship from instruction to
         the per-treasurer rows.

         CapitalBackend protocol with PrepareResponse / ExecuteResponse;
         StripeConnectBackend.from_env reads STRIPE_SECRET_KEY +
         STRIPE_CONNECT_ACCOUNT_ID + STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET (last is
         optional); BankTransferBackend.from_env reads MERCURY_API_TOKEN
         + MERCURY_API_BASE; verify_stripe_webhook_signature does
         constant-time HMAC-SHA-256 with a 5-minute skew check;
         backend_for_method factory returns the configured backend by
         preparation_method string.
  - NEW  server/fund/services/capital_deployment.py
         CapitalDeployment service with prepare / approve / execute /
         cancel methods. prepare() collapses on idempotency_key;
         approve() writes one TreasurerApproval row and transitions
         status to ``approved``; execute() enforces single-approval
         and (≥ DUAL_APPROVAL_THRESHOLD_USD) dual-approval gates

         POST /webhooks/stripe                (HMAC-signed body only)
         _gate() mirrors partner_api._attach_principal so the router
         operates outside the FundSecurityMiddleware path filter.
         Idempotency-Key header is forwarded to the service layer.

         + server/fund/schemas/events/investment_funded.v1.json

Prompt 51 prohibitions honored:
